      "df = analyser.track()\n",
      "param_cols = [\"Rt\", *cs.SIRF.PARAMETERS]\n",
      "oxcgrt_cols = oxcgrt_data.OXCGRT_VARS[:]\n",

      "delay = 14\n",
      "\n",
      "for col in param_cols:\n",
